      <div id="article-contents" class="article-grid-body"> 
       <h2 id="organization"><a href="#organization">Organization</a></h2> 
       <p>The Migrations API is only available to authenticated organization owners. For more information, see "<a href="/en/organizations/managing-peoples-access-to-your-organization-with-roles/permission-levels-for-an-organization#permission-levels-for-an-organization">Permission levels for an organization</a>" and "<a href="/en/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods">Other authentication methods</a>."</p> 
       <p>The organization migrations API lets you move a repository from GitHub to GitHub Enterprise Server.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-organization-migrations" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-organization-migrations">List organization migrations</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists the most recent migrations.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/migrations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-organization-migrations--parameters"> <a href="#list-organization-migrations--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#list-organization-migrations-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Exclude attributes from the API response to improve performance</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-organization-migrations--code-samples"> <a href="#list-organization-migrations--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/migrations</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /orgs/{org}/migrations'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">mediaType</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">previews</span>: [
      <span class="hljs-string">'wyandotte'</span>
    ]
  }
})
</code></pre>

         <h4 id="list-organization-migrations-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>To access the Migrations API, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>. 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="start-an-organization-migration" class="pt-3"> <a href="#start-an-organization-migration">Start an organization migration</a> </h3> 
         <p>Initiates the generation of a migration archive.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /orgs/{org}/migrations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="start-an-organization-migration--parameters"> <a href="#start-an-organization-migration--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repositories</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. A list of arrays indicating which repositories should be migrated.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>lock_repositories</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates whether repositories should be locked (to prevent manipulation) while migrating data.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude_attachments</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates whether attachments should be excluded from the migration (to reduce migration archive file size).</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="start-an-organization-migration--code-samples"> <a href="#start-an-organization-migration--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/migrations \
  -d '{"repositories":["repositories"]}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /orgs/{org}/migrations'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repositories</span>: [
    <span class="hljs-string">'repositories'</span>
  ]
})
</code></pre>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-organization-migration-status" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-organization-migration-status">Get an organization migration status</a> </h3> 
         <p>Fetches the status of a migration.</p> 
         <p>The <code>state</code> of a migration can be one of the following values:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>pending</code>, which means the migration hasn't started yet.</li> 
          <li><code>exporting</code>, which means the migration is in progress.</li> 
          <li><code>exported</code>, which means the migration finished successfully.</li> 
          <li><code>failed</code>, which means the migration failed.</li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/migrations/{migration_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-organization-migration-status--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-organization-migration-status--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#get-an-organization-migration-status-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>migration_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>migration_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Exclude attributes from the API response to improve performance</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h4 id="get-an-organization-migration-status-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>To access the Migrations API, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>. 
         </div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="download-an-organization-migration-archive" class="pt-3"> <a href="#download-an-organization-migration-archive">Download an organization migration archive</a> </h3> 
         <p>Fetches the URL to a migration archive.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/migrations/{migration_id}/archive</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="download-an-organization-migration-archive--parameters"> <a href="#download-an-organization-migration-archive--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#download-an-organization-migration-archive-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td>

         <h3 id="unlock-an-organization-repository" class="pt-3"> <a href="#unlock-an-organization-repository">Unlock an organization repository</a> </h3> 
         <p>Unlocks a repository that was locked for migration. You should unlock each migrated repository and <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/repos#delete-a-repository">delete them</a> when the migration is complete and you no longer need the source data.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /orgs/{org}/migrations/{migration_id}/repos/{repo_name}/lock</code></pre>

         <h4 id="list-repositories-in-an-organization-migration-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>To access the Migrations API, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>. 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <h2 id="source-imports"><a href="#source-imports">Source imports</a></h2> 
       <p>The Source Import API lets you start an import from a Git, Subversion, Mercurial, or Team Foundation Version Control source repository. This is the same functionality as the GitHub Importer. For more information, see "<a href="/en/github/importing-your-projects-to-github/importing-a-repository-with-github-importer">Importing a repository with GitHub Importer</a>."</p> 
       <p>A typical source import would start the import and then (optionally) update the authors and/or update the preference for using Git LFS if large files exist in the import. You can also create a webhook that listens for the <a href="/en/developers/webhooks-and-events/webhook-events-and-payloads#repository_import"><code>RepositoryImportEvent</code></a> to find out the status of the import.</p> 
       <p>A more detailed example can be seen in this diagram:</p> 
       <pre><code>+---------+                     +--------+                              +---------------------+
| Tooling |                     | GitHub |                              | Original Repository |
+---------+                     +--------+                              +---------------------+
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Start import                |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |  Download source data                        |
     |                              |---------------------------------------------&gt;|
     |                              |                        Begin streaming data  |
     |                              |&lt;---------------------------------------------|
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Get import progress         |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |       "status": "importing"  |                                              |
     |&lt;-----------------------------|                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Get commit authors          |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Map a commit author         |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |                       Finish streaming data  |
     |                              |&lt;---------------------------------------------|
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |  Rewrite commits with mapped authors         |
     |                              |------+                                       |
     |                              |      |                                       |
     |                              |&lt;-----+                                       |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |  Update repository on GitHub                 |
     |                              |------+                                       |
     |                              |      |                                       |
     |                              |&lt;-----+                                       |
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Map a commit author         |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |                              |  Rewrite commits with mapped authors         |
     |                              |------+                                       |
     |                              |      |                                       |
     |                              |&lt;-----+                                       |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |  Update repository on GitHub                 |
     |                              |------+                                       |
     |                              |      |                                       |
     |                              |&lt;-----+                                       |
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Get large files             |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |  opt_in to Git LFS           |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |                              |  Rewrite commits for large files             |
     |                              |------+                                       |
     |                              |      |                                       |
     |                              |&lt;-----+                                       |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |  Update repository on GitHub                 |
     |                              |------+                                       |
     |                              |      |                                       |
     |                              |&lt;-----+                                       |
     |                              |                                              |
     |  Get import progress         |                                              |
     |-----------------------------&gt;|                                              |
     |        "status": "complete"  |                                              |
     |&lt;-----------------------------|                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
     |                              |                                              |
</code></pre> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-import-status" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-import-status">Get an import status</a> </h3> 
         <p>View the progress of an import.</p> 
         <p><strong>Import status</strong></p> 
         <p>This section includes details about the possible values of the <code>status</code> field of the Import Progress response.</p> 
         <p>An import that does not have errors will progress through these steps:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>detecting</code> - the "detection" step of the import is in progress because the request did not include a <code>vcs</code> parameter. The import is identifying the type of source control present at the URL.</li> 
          <li><code>importing</code> - the "raw" step of the import is in progress. This is where commit data is fetched from the original repository. The import progress response will include <code>commit_count</code> (the total number of raw commits that will be imported) and <code>percent</code> (0 - 100, the current progress through the import).</li> 
          <li><code>mapping</code> - the "rewrite" step of the import is in progress. This is where SVN branches are converted to Git branches, and where author updates are applied. The import progress response does not include progress information.</li> 
          <li><code>pushing</code> - the "push" step of the import is in progress. This is where the importer updates the repository on GitHub. The import progress response will include <code>push_percent</code>, which is the percent value reported by <code>git push</code> when it is "Writing objects".</li> 
          <li><code>complete</code> - the import is complete, and the repository is ready on GitHub.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>If there are problems, you will see one of these in the <code>status</code> field:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>auth_failed</code> - the import requires authentication in order to connect to the original repository. To update authentication for the import, please see the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#update-an-import">Update an import</a> section.</li> 
          <li><code>error</code> - the import encountered an error. The import progress response will include the <code>failed_step</code> and an error message. Contact <a href="https://support.github.com/contact">GitHub Support</a> or <a href="https://premium.githubsupport.com">GitHub Premium Support</a> for more information.</li> 
          <li><code>detection_needs_auth</code> - the importer requires authentication for the originating repository to continue detection. To update authentication for the import, please see the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#update-an-import">Update an import</a> section.</li> 
          <li><code>detection_found_nothing</code> - the importer didn't recognize any source control at the URL. To resolve, <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#cancel-an-import">Cancel the import</a> and <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#start-an-import">retry</a> with the correct URL.</li> 
          <li><code>detection_found_multiple</code> - the importer found several projects or repositories at the provided URL. When this is the case, the Import Progress response will also include a <code>project_choices</code> field with the possible project choices as values. To update project choice, please see the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#update-an-import">Update an import</a> section.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p><strong>The project_choices field</strong></p> 
         <p>When multiple projects are found at the provided URL, the response hash will include a <code>project_choices</code> field, the value of which is an array of hashes each representing a project choice. The exact key/value pairs of the project hashes will differ depending on the version control type.</p> 
         <p><strong>Git LFS related fields</strong></p> 
         <p>This section includes details about Git LFS related fields that may be present in the Import Progress response.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>use_lfs</code> - describes whether the import has been opted in or out of using Git LFS. The value can be <code>opt_in</code>, <code>opt_out</code>, or <code>undecided</code> if no action has been taken.</li> 
          <li><code>has_large_files</code> - the boolean value describing whether files larger than 100MB were found during the <code>importing</code> step.</li> 
          <li><code>large_files_size</code> - the total size in gigabytes of files larger than 100MB found in the originating repository.</li> 
          <li><code>large_files_count</code> - the total number of files larger than 100MB found in the originating repository. To see a list of these files, make a "Get Large Files" request.</li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/import</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-import-status--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-import-status--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td>

         <h3 id="start-an-import" class="pt-3"> <a href="#start-an-import">Start an import</a> </h3> 
         <p>Start a source import to a GitHub repository using GitHub Importer.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/import</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="start-an-import--parameters"> <a href="#start-an-import--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>vcs_url</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The URL of the originating repository.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>vcs</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The originating VCS type. Can be one of <code>subversion</code>, <code>git</code>, <code>mercurial</code>, or <code>tfvc</code>. Please be aware that without this parameter, the import job will take additional time to detect the VCS type before beginning the import. This detection step will be reflected in the response.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>vcs_username</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>If authentication is required, the username to provide to <code>vcs_url</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>vcs_password</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>If authentication is required, the password to provide to <code>vcs_url</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>tfvc_project</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>For a tfvc import, the name of the project that is being imported.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        </div>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-commit-authors" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-commit-authors">Get commit authors</a> </h3> 
         <p>Each type of source control system represents authors in a different way. For example, a Git commit author has a display name and an email address, but a Subversion commit author just has a username. The GitHub Importer will make the author information valid, but the author might not be correct. For example, it will change the bare Subversion username <code>hubot</code> into something like <code>hubot &lt;hubot@12341234-abab-fefe-8787-fedcba987654&gt;</code>.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint and the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#map-a-commit-author">Map a commit author</a> endpoint allow you to provide correct Git author information.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/import/authors</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-commit-authors--parameters"> <a href="#get-commit-authors--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A user ID. Only return users with an ID greater than this ID.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="get-commit-authors--code-samples"> <a href="#get-commit-authors--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \

        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-git-lfs-preference" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-git-lfs-preference">Update Git LFS preference</a> </h3> 
         <p>You can import repositories from Subversion, Mercurial, and TFS that include files larger than 100MB. This ability is powered by <a href="https://git-lfs.github.com">Git LFS</a>. You can learn more about our LFS feature and working with large files <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/versioning-large-files/">on our help site</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/import/lfs</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-git-lfs-preference--parameters"> <a href="#update-git-lfs-preference--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>use_lfs</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. Can be one of <code>opt_in</code> (large files will be stored using Git LFS) or <code>opt_out</code> (large files will be removed during the import).</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="update-git-lfs-preference--code-samples"> <a href="#update-git-lfs-preference--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4>

  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \

  -d '{"use_lfs":"use_lfs"}'</code></pre>

       <h2 id="user"><a href="#user">User</a></h2> 
       <p>The User migrations API is only available to authenticated account owners. For more information, see "<a href="/en/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods">Other authentication methods</a>."</p> 
       <p>You can use this API to review, backup, or migrate your user data stored on GitHub.com. For a list of migration data that you can download, see "<a href="#download-a-user-migration-archive">Download a user migration archive</a>."</p> 
       <p>To download an archive, you'll need to start a user migration first. Once the status of the migration is <code>exported</code>, you can download the migration.</p> 
       <p>Once you've created a migration archive, it will be available to download for seven days. But, you can delete the user migration archive sooner if you'd like. You can unlock your repository when the migration is <code>exported</code> to begin using your repository again or delete the repository if you no longer need the source data.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-user-migrations" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-user-migrations">List user migrations</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists all migrations a user has started.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/migrations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-user-migrations--parameters"> <a href="#list-user-migrations--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#list-user-migrations-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h4>Not modified</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 304 Not Modified</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Requires authentication</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 401 Unauthorized</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Forbidden</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 403 Forbidden</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4 id="list-user-migrations-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>To access the Migrations API, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>. 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="start-a-user-migration" class="pt-3"> <a href="#start-a-user-migration">Start a user migration</a> </h3> 
         <p>Initiates the generation of a user migration archive.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /user/migrations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="start-a-user-migration--parameters"> <a href="#start-a-user-migration--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>lock_repositories</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Lock the repositories being migrated at the start of the migration</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude_attachments</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Do not include attachments in the migration</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Exclude attributes from the API response to improve performance</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repositories</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="start-a-user-migration--code-samples"> <a href="#start-a-user-migration--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/user/migrations \
  -d '{"repositories":["repositories"]}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /user/migrations'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">repositories</span>: [
    <span class="hljs-string">'repositories'</span>
  ]
})
</code></pre>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-a-user-migration-status" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-user-migration-status">Get a user migration status</a> </h3> 
         <p>Fetches a single user migration. The response includes the <code>state</code> of the migration, which can be one of the following values:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>pending</code> - the migration hasn't started yet.</li> 
          <li><code>exporting</code> - the migration is in progress.</li> 
          <li><code>exported</code> - the migration finished successfully.</li> 
          <li><code>failed</code> - the migration failed.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>Once the migration has been <code>exported</code> you can <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#download-a-user-migration-archive">download the migration archive</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/migrations/{migration_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-a-user-migration-status--parameters"> <a href="#get-a-user-migration-status--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#get-a-user-migration-status-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>migration_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>migration_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>exclude</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="get-a-user-migration-status--code-samples"> <a href="#get-a-user-migration-status--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/user/migrations/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /user/migrations/{migration_id}'</span>, {

    <span class="hljs-attr">previews</span>: [
      <span class="hljs-string">'wyandotte'</span>
    ]
  }
})

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="download-a-user-migration-archive" class="pt-3"> <a href="#download-a-user-migration-archive">Download a user migration archive</a> </h3> 
         <p>Fetches the URL to download the migration archive as a <code>tar.gz</code> file. Depending on the resources your repository uses, the migration archive can contain JSON files with data for these objects:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>attachments</li> 
          <li>bases</li> 
          <li>commit_comments</li> 
          <li>issue_comments</li> 
          <li>issue_events</li> 
          <li>issues</li> 
          <li>milestones</li> 
          <li>organizations</li> 
          <li>projects</li> 
          <li>protected_branches</li> 
          <li>pull_request_reviews</li> 
          <li>pull_requests</li> 
          <li>releases</li> 
          <li>repositories</li> 
          <li>review_comments</li> 
          <li>schema</li> 
          <li>users</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>The archive will also contain an <code>attachments</code> directory that includes all attachment files uploaded to GitHub.com and a <code>repositories</code> directory that contains the repository's Git data.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/migrations/{migration_id}/archive</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="download-a-user-migration-archive--parameters"> <a href="#download-a-user-migration-archive--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#download-a-user-migration-archive-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>migration_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>migration_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="download-a-user-migration-archive--code-samples"> <a href="#download-a-user-migration-archive--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/user/migrations/42/archive</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /user/migrations/{migration_id}/archive'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">migration_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">mediaType</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">previews</span>: [
      <span class="hljs-string">'wyandotte'</span>
    ]
  }
})
</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="delete-a-user-migration-archive" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-a-user-migration-archive">Delete a user migration archive</a> </h3> 
         <p>Deletes a previous migration archive. Downloadable migration archives are automatically deleted after seven days. Migration metadata, which is returned in the <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#list-user-migrations">List user migrations</a> and <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#get-a-user-migration-status">Get a user migration status</a> endpoints, will continue to be available even after an archive is deleted.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /user/migrations/{migration_id}/archive</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="delete-a-user-migration-archive--parameters"> <a href="#delete-a-user-migration-archive--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="unlock-a-user-repository" class="pt-3"> <a href="#unlock-a-user-repository">Unlock a user repository</a> </h3> 
         <p>Unlocks a repository. You can lock repositories when you <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/migrations#start-a-user-migration">start a user migration</a>. Once the migration is complete you can unlock each repository to begin using it again or <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/repos#delete-a-repository">delete the repository</a> if you no longer need the source data. Returns a status of <code>404 Not Found</code> if the repository is not locked.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /user/migrations/{migration_id}/repos/{repo_name}/lock</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="unlock-a-user-repository--parameters"> <a href="#unlock-a-user-repository--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

         <h3 id="list-repositories-for-a-user-migration" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-repositories-for-a-user-migration">List repositories for a user migration</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists all the repositories for this user migration.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/migrations/{migration_id}/repositories</code></pre>

            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#list-repositories-for-a-user-migration-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>migration_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>migration_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-repositories-for-a-user-migration--code-samples"> <a href="#list-repositories-for-a-user-migration--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.wyandotte-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/user/migrations/42/repositories</code></pre>

      <span class="hljs-string">'wyandotte'</span>

  }
})
